#[global] Unset Universe Checking.

(********************************************************************

 The Kleisli category

 The usual definition of the Kleisli category (given in the file
 `Monads.KleisliCategory.v` does not give rise to a univalent
 category. In this file, we give an alternative definition of the
 Kleisli category in such a way that we do get a univalent category.
 This definition can be found here:

 https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/Kleisli+category#in_terms_of_free_algebras

 We also prove its universal property.

 Note: to prove its universal property, we use that the usual
 definition of the Kleisli category (which is not necessarily
 univalent), satisfies the universal property. We also use that we
 have a weak equivalence between these two categories.

 Contents
 1. The free algebra functor
 2. The univalent Kleisli category
 3. The weak equivalence
 4. The universal property

 ********************************************************************)

 1. The free algebra functor

End FreeAlgebraFunctor.

(**
 2. The univalent Kleisli category
 *)
Definition kleisli_cat
           {C : category}
           (m : Monad C)
  : category
  := full_img_sub_precategory (free_alg_em m).

Definition univalent_kleisli_cat
           {C : univalent_category}
           (m : Monad C)
  : univalent_category
  := @univalent_image
       C
       (eilenberg_moore_univalent_cat C m)
       (free_alg_em m).

C: category

is_nat_trans (m ‚àô kleisli_incl m) (kleisli_incl m)
  ((Œª x : C,
    make_mor_eilenberg_moore m
      (Œº m x
       :
       C ‚ü¶ pr11 ((m ‚àô kleisli_incl m) x),
       pr11 (kleisli_incl m x) ‚üß)

       ¬∑ (Œº m x
          :
          C ‚ü¶ pr11 ((m ‚àô kleisli_incl m) x),
          pr11 (kleisli_incl m x) ‚üß) =

         (Œº m x

          C ‚ü¶ pr11 ((m ‚àô kleisli_incl m) x),
          pr11 (kleisli_incl m x) ‚üß)
       ¬∑ pr21 (kleisli_incl m x)),, tt)
   :
   nat_trans_data (m ‚àô kleisli_incl m)
     (kleisli_incl m))
 abstract
      (intros x y f ;
       use eq_mor_kleisli_cat ; cbn ;
       apply (nat_trans_ax (Œº m))).
Defined.

(**
 3. The weak equivalence
 *)

‚Üí kleisli_cat m ‚ü¶ ?F a, ?F b ‚üß

z_iso (free_alg_em m x) (free_alg_em m x)

    apply identity_z_iso.

m: Monad C
‚àè a b : Kleisli_cat_monad m,
Kleisli_cat_monad m ‚ü¶ a, b ‚üß
‚Üí kleisli_cat m
  ‚ü¶ (Œª x : Kleisli_cat_monad m,
     free_alg_em m x,,
     hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x))) a,
  (Œª x : Kleisli_cat_monad m,
   free_alg_em m x,,
   hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x))) b ‚üß

eilenberg_moore_cat m
‚ü¶ free_alg_em m x,,
  hinhpr (x,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m x)),
free_alg_em m y,,
hinhpr (y,, identity_z_iso (free_alg_em m y)) ‚üß

    
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad m

Œ∑ m (m y) ¬∑ Œº m y = ?t2

      apply Monad_law1.
    
C: category
m: Monad C
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad m
f: kleisli_cat m ‚ü¶ functor_to_kleisli_cat m x,
functor_to_kleisli_cat m y ‚üß
œà‚ÇÅ, œà‚ÇÇ: hfiber
  (Œª f : Kleisli_cat_monad m ‚ü¶ x, y ‚üß,
   # (functor_to_kleisli_cat m) f) f
p:= pr2 œà‚ÇÅ @ ! pr2 œà‚ÇÇ: make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (# m (pr1 œà‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Œº m y)
  (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data_subproof C m x y
     (pr1 œà‚ÇÅ)),, tt =
make_mor_eilenberg_moore m (# m (pr1 œà‚ÇÇ) ¬∑ Œº m y)
  (functor_to_kleisli_cat_data_subproof C m x y
     (pr1 œà‚ÇÇ)),, tt
q: Œ∑ m x ¬∑ # m (pr1 œà‚ÇÅ) ¬∑ Œº m y =
Œ∑ m x ¬∑ # m (pr1 œà‚ÇÇ) ¬∑ Œº m y
pr1 œà‚ÇÇ ¬∑ identity (m y) = pr1 œà‚ÇÇ

    apply id_right.
Qed.

(**
 4. The universal property
 *)
Section KleisliUMP1.
  Context {C‚ÇÅ C‚ÇÇ : univalent_category}
          (m : Monad C‚ÇÅ)
          (F : C‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ C‚ÇÇ)
          (Œ≥ : m ‚àô F ‚üπ F)
          (p‚ÇÅ : ‚àè (x : C‚ÇÅ), #F (Œ∑ m x) ¬∑ Œ≥ x = identity _)
          (p‚ÇÇ : ‚àè (x : C‚ÇÅ), Œ≥ _ ¬∑ Œ≥ x = #F (Œº m x) ¬∑ Œ≥ x).

  Definition functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat
    : kleisli_cat m ‚ü∂ C‚ÇÇ
    := lift_functor_along
         C‚ÇÇ
         (functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (essentially_surjective_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (fully_faithful_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad m F Œ≥ p‚ÇÅ p‚ÇÇ).

  Definition functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_nat_trans
    : kleisli_incl m ‚àô functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat ‚üπ F
    := nat_trans_comp
         _ _ _
         (nat_trans_comp
            _ _ _
            (post_whisker
               (functor_to_kleisli_cat_incl_nat_z_iso m)
               functor_from_univalent_kleisli_cat)
            (pre_whisker
               _
               (lift_functor_along_comm
                  C‚ÇÇ
                  (functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
                  (essentially_surjective_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
                  (fully_faithful_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
                  (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad m F Œ≥ p‚ÇÅ p‚ÇÇ))))
         (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad_nat_trans m F Œ≥ p‚ÇÅ p‚ÇÇ).

            _).

  Definition nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat
    : G‚ÇÅ ‚üπ G‚ÇÇ
    := lift_nat_trans_along
         C‚ÇÇ
         (functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (essentially_surjective_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (fully_faithful_functor_to_kleisli_cat m)
         (nat_trans_from_kleisli_cat_monad
            m
            nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help
            nat_trans_from_univalent_kleisli_cat_help_eq).
